war_measures = {
	GER_Oster_Conspiracy_WW2 = {
		icon = TBI
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			controls_state = 806
			controls_state = 1498
			controls_state = 42
			controls_state = 51
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 90
		is_good = no
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_war_support = 0.25
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Oster_Coup.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

economy_decisions = {
	###########################
	# Rebuild Grozny Oilfields
	###########################
	GER_Rebuild_Grozny_Oilfields = {
		fire_only_once = yes
		icon = GFX_decision_oil
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = RKA
			}
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				GER = {
					controls_state = 232
				}
				RKA = {
					controls_state = 232
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = SOV_Destroyed_Grozny
			OR = {
				GER = {
					controls_state = 232
				}
				RKA = {
					controls_state = 232
				}
			}
		}
		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
		days_remove = 180
		cost = 20
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 232
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}
		remove_effect = {
			add_resource = {
				type = oil
				amount = 20
				state = 232
			}

GER_Reichsautobahn_category = {
	###########################
	# Reichsautobahn - Berlin
	###########################
	GER_Reichsautobahn_Berlin = {
		icon = GFX_decision_GER_Reichsautobahn_icon
		fire_only_once = yes
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				amount_of_money_to_check = 200
			}
			has_specific_amount_of_money_with_inflation_included = yes
		}
		custom_cost_text = GER_Reichsautobahn_cost
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 64
			}
		}
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			has_start_date < 1936.01.01
			has_completed_focus = GER_Reichsautobahn
		}
		available = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				amount_of_money_to_check = 200
			}
			has_specific_amount_of_money_with_inflation_included = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = GER_Reichsautobahn_in_Construction
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_Reichsautobahn_in_Construction
				}
			}
			has_full_control_of_state = 64
			has_full_control_of_state = 1057
		}
		cost = 50
		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 5
			production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.05
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		days_remove = 140
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				money_to_gain = -200
			}
			add_money_with_inflation_included_with_tooltip_effect = yes
			news_event = {
				id = GER_Reichsautobahn.1
				hours = 6
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_Reichsautobahn_in_Construction
		}
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				unemployment_value = -0.005
			}
			add_unemployment_effect = yes
			clr_country_flag = GER_Reichsautobahn_in_Construction
			64 = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 5
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			1057 = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 5
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}

				limit = {
					798 = {

							tag = POL
							has_civil_war = no
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {

							has_government = fascist
						}
					}

						annex_country = {
							target = DNZ
							transfer_troops = no
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					effect_tooltip = {
						declare_war_on = {
							target = DNZ
							type = take_state
							generator = {
								85
							}
						}
					}
				}
				POL = {
					country_event = {
						id = GER_Danzig_or_War.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				archetype = CV_equipment
				size > 3
			}
			has_navy_size = {
				archetype = CA_equipment
				size > 14
			}
			has_navy_size = {
				archetype = CL_equipment
				size > 12
			}
			has_navy_size = {
				archetype = DD_equipment
				size > 13
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 3285
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = GER_Plan_Z

					92 = {
						set_building_level = {
							type = air_base
							level = 2
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					92 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = air_base
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					79 = {
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						79 = {
							air_base < 2
						}
					}
					79 = {
						set_building_level = {
							type = air_base
							level = 6
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					79 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = air_base
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_Prepared_forward_Luftwaffe_Airfields
		}

## Third Versailles
#########################
GER_Third_Versailles_category = {
	#########################
	## Dictate to England
	#########################
	GER_Dictate_Terms_to_England = {
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = GER_Third_Versailles_Dictates
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = ENG
			}
		}
		cost = 25
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Third_Versailles.5
			}
		}
	}
	#########################
	## Dictate to France
	#########################
	GER_Dictate_Terms_to_France = {
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = GER_Third_Versailles_Dictates
			is_Nazi_Germany = yes
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FRA
			}
		}
		cost = 25
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = GER_Third_Versailles.10
			}
		}
	}
	##########################
	## Finalise the Treaty
	##########################
	GER_Finalise_Versailles_Treaty = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = GER_French_Terms_Dictated
			has_country_flag = GER_English_Terms_Dictated
			is_Nazi_Germany = yes
		}
		available = {
			
		}
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		complete_effect = {
			add_ideas = GER_Triumphant_Will
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = {
					id = GER_Third_Versailles.14
				}
			}
		}
	}
